<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top" align="left"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#160;2.02.</span></td>
<td align="left" style="vertical-align:top"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Results of Operations and Financial Condition. </p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On November&#160;5, 2020, iCAD, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) issued a press release announcing its financial results for the quarter ended September&#160;30, 2020. A copy of the Company&#8217;s press release is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1 and is incorporated herein by reference. </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>
<table style="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;border:0;width:100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid">
<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top" align="left"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#160;9.01</span></td>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>iCAD REPORTS FINANCIAL RESULTS FOR THIRD QUARTER AND NINE MONTHS ENDED </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>SEPTEMBER&nbsp;30, 2020 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Achieved Sequential Revenue Growth of 28% in Third Quarter of 2020, Driven by Detection </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Product and Therapy Product Revenue Growth of 44% and 251%, Respectively </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Net Loss Improved by $1.2&nbsp;million to $1.8&nbsp;million in the Third Quarter of 2020 as Compared to </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>$3.0&nbsp;million in the Third Quarter of 2019 </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>New AI Offering Expands Focus from Current Age Based Detection to 2 Year Risk Assessment </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>and Personalized Screening Regimen </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>New Partnership Agreement Enhances Commercial Access to Enterprise and Integrated </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Delivery Systems </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Conference Call Today at 4:30 p.m. ET </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>NASHUA, N.H. &#150; November</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;5, 2020 &#150;</B> iCAD, Inc. (NASDAQ: ICAD),&nbsp;a global medical technology leader providing innovative
cancer detection and therapy solutions, today reported its financial and operating results for the three and nine months ended September&nbsp;30, 2020. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Recent Highlights: </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">ProFound AI Risk, the first and only commercially available clinical decision support tool providing accurate <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">two-year</FONT> breast cancer risk estimation personalized for each woman, currently available on an introductory basis for 2D mammography in the U.S. and Europe </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Data published recently in the peer-reviewed journal, <I>Radiology</I>, showed that our technology significantly
outperformed existing breast cancer risk models </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Signed distribution agreement with Change Healthcare, a leading independent healthcare technology company focused
on insights, innovation and accelerating the transformation of the U.S. healthcare system, that will expand access to ProFound AI<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&#153;</SUP> for more hospitals and imaging centers across North America
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Presented updated positive clinical data for Xoft<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> Brain
IORT demonstrating significant improvement in overall survival and local progression-free survival in patients with recurrent GBM treated with Xoft versus patients treated with external beam radiation therapy and systemic therapy
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Cash balance of $22.6&nbsp;million at the end of the third quarter of 2020 </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Our third quarter 2020 total revenue of $7.1&nbsp;million represented sequential growth of 28&nbsp;percent as compared to the second quarter and we
achieved over 44% sequential growth in AI product revenue in the third quarter, as ProFound AI continues to gain traction in the market. Further, we demonstrated sequential growth of over 250% in Xoft product revenue during the third quarter. Our
third quarter revenue growth was achieved while holding operating expenses essentially flat on a sequential basis, and we reduced our net loss to $1.8&nbsp;million which is an improvement of $0.6&nbsp;million on a sequential basis and
$1.2&nbsp;million as compared to the third quarter of 2019,&#148; said Mike Klein, Chairman and CEO. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Looking ahead, we are extremely excited about
the commercial potential of ProFound AI Risk, a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">first-in-kind</FONT></FONT> solution that provides crucial data about patients&#146; individual risk of developing breast cancer
between screenings and empowers clinicians to truly personalize patient care,&#148; continued Mr.&nbsp;Klein. &#147;ProFound AI Risk is currently available on an introductory basis for 2D mammography and we expect will subsequently be available for
the rapidly growing 3D mammography market. We were also thrilled to announce our recent distribution agreement with Change Healthcare, which will provide more seamless <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">on-demand</FONT> AI access, significant clinical
utility, and an anywhere, anytime <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pay-per-use</FONT></FONT> recurring revenue solution with even greater revenue predictability in the future. Enterprise imaging partners, like
Change, will be an increasingly potent distribution channel for iCAD, and a complement to both our direct sales and our <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">OEM-channel</FONT> partners.&#148; </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Based on the encouraging data generated to date that show the feasibility of Xoft to treat recurrent
glioblastomas, we intend to initiate a Phase 2 clinical trial in this high-value indication by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-end.</FONT> This multi-center study will enroll <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">80-100</FONT> patients over an
approximately <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">two-year</FONT> period, with early progression-free survival data potentially available in one year,&#148; concluded Mr. Klein. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Third quarter 2020 Financial Results </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Revenue: Cancer
Detection revenue for the third quarter of 2020, which includes the Company&#146;s mammography and breast density products, and the associated service and supplies revenue, decreased by approximately $0.8&nbsp;million, or 13%, as compared to the
third quarter of 2019. Therapy revenue for the third quarter of 2020, which includes Xoft<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> Axxent<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> eBx<SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> System<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> sales, as well as the associated service and supplies revenue, increased by $0.1&nbsp;million, or 4%, as compared to the third
quarter of 2019. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Total Detection and Therapy revenue for the third quarter of 2020 was $7.1&nbsp;million, a decrease of $0.7&nbsp;million, or 9%,
compared to the third quarter of 2019, reflecting a 12% decrease in product revenue, and a 4% decrease in service and supplies revenue. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating Expenses: Total operating expenses for the third quarter of 2020 were $6.7&nbsp;million, a
$1.3&nbsp;million, or 16%, decrease from $8.0&nbsp;million in the third quarter of 2019. The decrease was driven by expense controls implemented during the second quarter. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">GAAP Net Loss: Net loss for the third quarter of 2020 was ($1.8) million, or ($0.08) per diluted share, compared with a net loss of ($3.0) million, or ($0.15)
per diluted share, for the third quarter of 2019. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted Net loss:
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> adjusted net loss, a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure as defined below, for the third quarter of 2020 was ($1.7) million, or ($0.07) per diluted share, as compared to
a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjusted net loss of ($2.0) million, or ($0.10) per diluted share, for the third quarter of 2019. Please refer to the section entitled &#147;Reconciliation of
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures to Comparable GAAP Measures&#148; and the accompanying financial table included at the end of this release for a reconciliation of GAAP Net Loss to
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted Net Loss results for the three-month periods ended September&nbsp;30, 2020 and 2019, respectively. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA: <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> adjusted EBITDA, a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure as defined below, for the third quarter of 2020 was a loss of ($1.0) million, a $0.4&nbsp;million decrease compared to the third quarter 2019
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjusted EBITDA loss of ($1.4) million. Please refer to the section entitled &#147;Reconciliation of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures to Comparable GAAP
Measures&#148; and the accompanying financial table included at the end of this release for a reconciliation of GAAP Net Loss to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA results for the three-month periods ended
September&nbsp;30, 2020 and 2019, respectively. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Nine months ended September&nbsp;30, 2020 Financial Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Revenue: Total Detection and Therapy revenue for the nine months ended September&nbsp;30, 2020 was $19.2&nbsp;million, a decrease of $2.7&nbsp;million, or 12%,
compared to the same period of 2019, reflecting a 16% decrease in product revenue, and a 7% decrease in service and supplies revenue. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

compared to $17.1&nbsp;million, or 77% of revenue, in the same period of 2019. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating Expenses: Total operating expenses for the nine months ended
September&nbsp;30, 2020 were $21.8&nbsp;million, a $0.3&nbsp;million, or 1%, increase from $21.5&nbsp;million in the same period of 2019. The increase was driven by increases in marketing and G&amp;A expense during the first quarter of 2020, offset
by decreases in the second and third quarters as a result of expense controls implemented during the second and third quarters of 2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">GAAP Net Loss:
Net loss for the nine months ended September&nbsp;30, 2020 was ($16.0) million, or ($0.73) per diluted share, compared with a net loss of ($10.2) million, or ($0.57) per diluted share, for the same period of 2019. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted Net loss: <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> adjusted net loss, a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure as defined below, for the nine months ended September&nbsp;30, 2020 was ($8.1) million, or ($0.37) per diluted share, as compared to a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT>
adjusted net loss of ($4.7) million, or ($0.27) per diluted share, for the same period of 2019. Please refer to the section entitled &#147;Reconciliation of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures to Comparable GAAP
Measures&#148; and the accompanying financial table included at the end of this release for a reconciliation of GAAP Net Loss to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted Net Loss results for the nine month periods ended
September&nbsp;30, 2020 and 2019, respectively. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA:
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> adjusted EBITDA, a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure as defined below, for the first nine months of 2020 was a loss of ($4.8) million, a $1.8&nbsp;million increase
compared to the third quarter 2019 <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjusted EBITDA loss of ($3.0) million. Please refer to the section entitled &#147;Reconciliation of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial
Measures to Comparable GAAP Measures&#148; and the accompanying financial table included at the end of this release for a reconciliation of GAAP Net Loss to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA results for the nine month
periods ended September&nbsp;30, 2020 and 2019, respectively. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Cash and Cash Equivalents: As of September&nbsp;30, 2020, the Company had cash and cash
equivalents of $22.6&nbsp;million, compared to cash and cash equivalents of $15.3&nbsp;million at December&nbsp;31, 2019. In April 2020, the Company closed a registered direct offering for net proceeds of approximately $12.3&nbsp;million. </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Reconciliation of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures to Comparable GAAP
Measures </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company reports its financial results in accordance with United States generally accepted accounting principles, or GAAP. However,
management believes that in order to understand the Company&#146;s short-term and long-term financial and operational trends, investors may wish to consider the impact of certain <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> or <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</FONT> items, when used as a supplement to financial performance measures in accordance with GAAP. These items result from facts and circumstances that vary in frequency and/or impact on continuing
operations. Management also uses results of operations before such items to evaluate the operating performance of the Company and compare it against past periods, make operating decisions, and serve as a basis for strategic planning. These <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provide management with additional means to understand and evaluate the operating results and trends in the Company&#146;s ongoing business by eliminating certain <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> expenses and other items that management believes might otherwise make comparisons of the Company&#146;s ongoing business with prior periods more difficult, obscure trends in ongoing operations or reduce
management&#146;s ability to make useful forecasts. Management believes that these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provide additional means of evaluating period-over-period operating performance. In addition,
management understands that some investors and financial analysts find this information helpful in analyzing the Company&#146;s financial and operational performance and comparing this performance to its peers and competitors. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Management defines <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#147;Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA&#148; as the sum of GAAP Net Loss before provisions for interest
expense, other income, stock-based compensation expense, depreciation and amortization, tax expense, severance, gain on sale of assets, loss on disposal of assets, acquisition and litigation related expenses. Management considers this <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure to be an indicator of the Company&#146;s operational strength and performance of its business and a good measure of its historical operating trends, in particular the extent to which
ongoing operations impact the Company&#146;s overall financial performance. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures do
not replace the presentation of the Company&#146;s GAAP financial results and should only be used as a supplement to, not as a substitute for, the Company&#146;s financial results presented in accordance with GAAP. The Company has provided a
reconciliation of each <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure used in its financial reporting and investor presentations to the most directly comparable GAAP financial measure. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Management excludes each of the items identified below from the applicable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure referenced above
for the reasons set forth with respect to that excluded item: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Interest expense: The Company excludes interest expense which includes interest from the facility agreement,
interest on capital leases and interest on the convertible debentures from its <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA calculation. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Stock-based compensation expense: excluded as these are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> expenses
that management does not consider part of ongoing operating results when assessing the performance of the Company&#146;s business, and also because the total amount of expense is partially outside of the Company&#146;s control as it is based on
factors such as stock price volatility and interest rates, which may be unrelated to our performance during the period in which the expense is incurred. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Amortization and Depreciation: Purchased assets and intangibles are amortized over a period of several years and
generally cannot be changed or influenced by management after they are acquired. Accordingly, these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> items are not considered by management in making operating decisions, and management believes that
such expenses do not have a direct correlation to future business operations. Thus, including such charges does not accurately reflect the performance of the Company&#146;s ongoing operations for the period in which such charges are incurred.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Severance and furlough relates to costs incurred due to the termination of certain employees. The Company
provides compensation to certain employees as an accommodation upon termination of employment without cause. Management believes that excluding severance and furlough costs from operating results provides investors with a better means for measuring
current Company performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Loss on fair value of convertible debentures. The Company excludes this
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> item as it is not considered by management in making operating decisions, and management believes that such item does not have a direct correlation to future business operations.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Acquisition related: relates to professional service fees associated with acquisitions. The Company does not
consider these acquisition-related costs to be related to the organic continuing operations of the acquired businesses and are generally not relevant to assessing or estimating the long-term performance of the acquired assets. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

litigation. The Company excludes these costs from its <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures primarily because the Company believes that these costs have no direct correlation to the core operations of the Company.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On occasion in the future, there may be other items, such as loss on extinguishment of debt, the Cares tax credit, significant asset
impairments, restructuring charges or significant gains or losses from contingencies that the Company may exclude if it believes that doing so is consistent with the goal of providing useful information to investors and management. </P>
